<FILENAME>fortunanrjuly152015.htm
<DESCRIPTION>NEWS RELEASE DATED JULY 15, 2015
<TEXT>
<!doctype html public "-//IETF//DTD HTML//EN">
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Fortuna News Release</TITLE>
<META NAME="author" CONTENT="Jorge Alberto Ganoza">
<META NAME="date" CONTENT="07/15/2015">
</HEAD>
<BODY style="margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt; 
color:#000000">
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=center><img src="fortunanrjuly152015001.jpg" 
alt="[fortunanrjuly152015001.jpg]" align=middle height=116.867 width=1049.4></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=center><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:13pt" align=center><B>Fortuna reports production
of 1.7 million ounces of silver and 9,032 ounces of gold for the second quarter 
2015</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify><B>Vancouver, July 15, 
2015--</B> <B>Fortuna Silver Mines Inc. (NYSE: FSM) (TSX: FVI) </B>is pleased to
announce second quarter production figures from its two operating mines in Latin
America, the San Jose Mine in Mexico and the Caylloma Mine in Peru. &nbsp;The 
company produced 1.7 million ounces of silver, 9,032 ounces of gold and 
significant base metal by-products. &nbsp;Silver and gold production for the 
first six months of the year totaled 3.3 million and 18,771 ounces respectively;
reflecting 51 percent and 53 percent of the company&#146;s annual guidance (see 
<FONT style="color:#0000FF"><U>Fortuna news release dated January 15, 
2015</U></FONT>). &nbsp;Fortuna is on schedule to produce 6.5 million ounces of 
silver and 35.3 thousand ounces of gold or 8.6 million ounces of Ag Eq* in 
2015.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>&#147;Consolidated 
production results for the first semester are in line with budget,&#148; 
commented Jorge A. Ganoza, President and CEO. &nbsp;&#147;At Caylloma, 
operational issues at level 6 of Animas caused lower silver production in the 
second quarter. &nbsp;For the remainder of the year, flexibility in the mine 
plan allows mining to focus on higher base metal-rich levels of the mine 
resulting in an increase in base metal production. &nbsp;Outperformance at San 
Jose, due to excess processing capacity and better head grades, will account for
the drop in silver production at Caylloma.&#148; &nbsp;Mr. Ganoza continued, 
&#147;We are on track to meet our annual production guidance.&#148;</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify><B><I>Second Quarter 
Production Highlights:</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:24px; width:48px; 
font-family:Wingdings; font-size:11pt; float:left">&#167;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Silver production of 1,671,309 ounces; 3 % increase over Q2 
2014</P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:24px; width:48px; 
font-family:Wingdings; font-size:11pt; clear:left; float:left">&#167;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Gold production of 9,032 ounces; 6 % increase over Q2 2014</P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:24px; width:48px; 
font-family:Wingdings; font-size:11pt; clear:left; float:left">&#167;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Lead production of 4,770,470 pounds; 20 % increase over Q2 
2014</P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:24px; width:48px; 
font-family:Wingdings; font-size:11pt; clear:left; float:left">&#167;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Zinc production of 8,574,831 pounds; 28 % increase over Q2 
2014</P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:24px; width:48px; 
font-family:Wingdings; font-size:11pt; clear:left; float:left">&#167;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Cash cost** for the San Jose Mine is US$58.0 /t; on track to meet 
annual guidance of US$62.7/t</P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:24px; width:48px; 
font-family:Wingdings; font-size:11pt; clear:left; float:left">&#167;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Cash cost** for the Caylloma Mine is US$88.6 /t; on track to meet 
annual guidance of US$90.3/t</P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:8pt">* &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Ag Eq is 
calculated using silver to gold ratio of 60 to 1</P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:8pt">** &nbsp;&nbsp;Preliminary estimates of 
cash operating costs per tonne, subject to modification on final cost 
consolidation </P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>

Highlights:</I></B></P>

font-size:11pt">Production (lbs)</P>

</TD><TD style="margin-top:0px; border-right:1px solid #000000; border-

style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:11pt">&nbsp;</P></TD><TD

</TABLE>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify><B>San Jose Mine, 
Mexico</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Silver and gold production 
for the second quarter were 10 % and 3 % above budget, respectively. 
&nbsp;Average head grades for silver and gold were 228 g/t and 1.62 g/t or 4 % 
above and 2 % below budget, respectively. &nbsp;Metallurgical recoveries for 
silver and gold were 91.57 % and 91.06 % or 2.9 % and 2.3 % above budget, 
respectively. </P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Annual silver production is 
projected to be above budget reflecting a 3 to 5 % increase in throughput and an
increase in head grade relative to the annual mine plan.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify><B>Caylloma Mine, 
Peru</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Silver production for the 
second quarter was 25 % below budget with an average silver head grade of 144 
g/t, 24&nbsp;% below plan. &nbsp;Metallurgical recovery for silver was 
82.33&nbsp;% or 2.3 % below budget.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Silver production for the 
semester was&nbsp;14&nbsp;% below budget due to higher than expected internal 
dilution as well as adverse geotechnical conditions which limited achieving 
programmed tonnage in Level 6 of the Animas Vein. &nbsp;To offset the Level 6 
production issues, mining was shifted to more base metal-rich levels within the 
Animas Vein resulting in higher than budgeted grades for lead and zinc. 
&nbsp;This strategy will continue to be implemented throughout the balance of 
the year projecting a decrease in production of 14 % in silver ounces and an 
increase of 12 % in zinc production. </P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Caylloma&#146;s revised 
production guidance for 2015 is 1.9&nbsp;million ounces of silver, 
19.5&nbsp;million pounds of lead and 32.1&nbsp;million pounds of zinc.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>The company reiterates its 
annual silver and gold production guidance of 6.5 million ounces of silver and 
35.3 thousand ounces of gold. &nbsp;For the second half of 2015, an increase in 
silver production of 0.3&nbsp;million ounces, has been budgeted at San Jose to 
account for the change in strategy at Caylloma. </P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify><B><I>Qualified Person 
</I></B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Boris G. Caro is a technical
consultant and a Qualified Person for Fortuna Silver Mines Inc. as defined by
National Instrument 43-101. &nbsp;Mr. Caro is a Member of Australasian Institute
of Mining and Metallurgy (Membership Number 305462) and a Registered Member of 
the Chilean Mining Commission (Comisi&#243;n Calificadora de Competencias en 
Recursos y Reservas Mineras, Registered Member Number 0229) and is responsible 
for ensuring that the information contained in this news release is an accurate 
summary of the original reports and data provided to or developed by Fortuna 
Silver Mines.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify><B><I>About Fortuna Silver 
Mines Inc.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:11pt" align=justify>Fortuna is a growth 
oriented, silver and base metal producer focused on mining opportunities in 
Latin America. &nbsp;Our primary assets are the Caylloma silver mine in southern
Peru and the San Jose silver-gold mine in Mexico. &nbsp;The company is 
selectively pursuing acquisition opportunities throughout the Americas. 
&nbsp;For more information, please visit our website at <FONT 
style="color:#0000FF"><U>www.fortunasilver.com</U></FONT>. </P>
